# Introduction

Identity and constant function.

  - ``∅ , 1 ∙ "x" ⦂ A  ⊢ ` "x" ⦂ A``
  - ``∅ ⊢ (ƛ "x" ⇒ ` "x") ⦂ [ 1 ∙ A ]⊸ A``
  - ``∅ , 1 ∙ "x" ⦂ A , 0 ∙ "y" ⦂ B ⊢ ` "x" ⦂ A``
  - ``∅ ⊢ (ƛ "x" ⇒ ƛ "y" ⇒ ` "x") ⦂ [ 1 ∙ A ]⊸ [ 0 ∙ B ]⊸ A``

Some numbers.

  - ``∅ , 1 ∙ "z" ⦂ ℕ , 0 ∙ "s" ⦂ [ 1 ∙ ℕ ]⊸ ℕ ⊢ ` "z" ⦂ ℕ``
  - ``∅ , 1 ∙ "z" ⦂ ℕ , 1 ∙ "s" ⦂ [ 1 ∙ ℕ ]⊸ ℕ ⊢ (` "s" · ` "z") ⦂ ℕ``
  - ``∅ , 1 ∙ "z" ⦂ ℕ , ω ∙ "s" ⦂ [ 1 ∙ ℕ ]⊸ ℕ ⊢ (` "s" · (` "s" · ` "z")) ⦂ ℕ``

Words.

    data Mult : Set where
      0# : Mult
      1# : Mult
      ω# : Mult

# Properties of Vector Operations

Unit scaling does nothing.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="**-identityˡ"></a><a id="3566" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#3566" class="Function">**-identityˡ</a> <a id="3579" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3581" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="3583" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3584" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#3584" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="3585" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3587" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3588" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#3588" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="3590" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3592" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#1911" class="Datatype">Context</a> <a id="3600" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#3584" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="3601" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="3606" class="Comment">-------------</a>

Scaling by a product is the composition of scalings.

Scaling the 0-vector gives the 0-vector.

Scaling by 0 gives the 0-vector.

Vector addition is commutative.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="⋈-comm"></a><a id="5202" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#5202" class="Function">⋈-comm</a> <a id="5209" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5211" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="5213" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5214" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#5214" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="5215" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5217" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5218" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#5218" class="Bound">Γ₁</a> <a id="5221" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#5221" class="Bound">Γ₂</a> <a id="5224" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5226" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#1911" class="Datatype">Context</a> <a id="5234" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#5214" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="5235" class="Symbol">)</a>

Vector addition is associative.

Scaling by a sum gives the sum of the scalings.

Scaling a sum gives the sum of the scalings.

  <a id="7090" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4239" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Linear maps preserve the 0-vector.

Adding a row of 0s to the end of the matrix and then multiplying by a vector produces a vector with a 0 at the bottom.

Linear maps preserve scaling.

Multiplying by a standard basis vector projects out the corresponding column of the matrix.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="⊛-identityˡ"></a><a id="10522" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#10522" class="Function">⊛-identityˡ</a> <a id="10534" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10536" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="10538" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10539" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#10539" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="10541" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#10541" class="Bound">δ</a><a id="10542" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10544" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10545" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#10545" class="Bound">A</a><a id="10546" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10548" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10549" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#10549" class="Bound">Ξ</a> <a id="10551" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10553" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#2637" class="Function">Matrix</a> <a id="10560" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#10539" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="10562" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#10541" class="Bound">δ</a><a id="10563" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="10568" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10570" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10571" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#10571" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="10573" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10575" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#10539" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="10577" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#1729" class="Datatype Operator">∋</a> <a id="10579" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#10545" class="Bound">A</a><a id="10580" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="10584" class="Comment">-----------------------</a>

  <a id="11176" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4239" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The standard basis vectors put together give the identity matrix.

# Simultaneous Substitution

Extend a matrix as the identity matrix -- add a zero to the end of every row, and add a new row with a 1 and the rest 0s.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="extm"></a><a id="13936" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#13936" class="Function">extm</a> <a id="13941" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13943" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="13945" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13946" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#13946" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="13948" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#13948" class="Bound">δ</a><a id="13949" class="Symbol">}</a>
